    int i, j, k;

        for (j = i + fold_len; j > i && line[j] != ' ' && line[j] != '\t'; j--) {
            // Find the nearest space or tab to break the line
        }
        
        if (j == i) {
            j = i + fold_len; // No space or tab found, fold at max_line_len
        }

        for (k = max_line_len - 1; k > j; k--) {

    }
